<a id="4448" class="Comment">{- Definition 19.1.3. Given a cocone structure on X and a family of maps indexed
   by X, we obtain a morphism of descent data. -}</a>

   morphisms equipped with two-sided inverses are equivalences. -}</a>

  <a id="15111" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15113" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15113" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="15115" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15117" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#1497" class="Function">hom-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="15133" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15058" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15135" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15083" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="15136" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15138" class="Symbol">→</a>

<a id="15197" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#14933" class="Function">equiv-is-equiv-hom-Fam-pushout</a> <a id="15228" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15228" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15230" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15230" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="15232" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15232" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="15234" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15234" class="Bound">is-equiv-h</a> <a id="15245" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="15249" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a>
    <a id="15258" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15260" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15262" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15262" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="15264" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15266" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="15271" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15272" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15276" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15232" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="15278" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15262" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15279" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15281" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15282" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15286" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15234" class="Bound">is-equiv-h</a> <a id="15297" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15262" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15298" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="15305" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15307" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a>
      <a id="15318" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15320" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="15322" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15322" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="15324" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15326" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="15331" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15332" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="15336" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15337" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15341" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15232" class="Bound">h</a><a id="15342" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15344" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15322" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15345" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15347" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15348" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15352" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15234" class="Bound">is-equiv-h</a> <a id="15363" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15322" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15364" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="15373" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="15375" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15380" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="15384" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.26-id-pushout.html#15232" class="Bound">h</a><a id="15385" class="Symbol">)))</a>

<a id="15390" class="Comment">{- Theorem 19.1.3. Characterization of identity types of pushouts. -}</a>

<a id="15461" class="Comment">{-
hom-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout :
  { l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l5}
  { f : S → A} {g : S → B} (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( up-X : (l : Level) → universal-property-pushout l f g c) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l4 f g) (a : A) (p : pr1 P a) →
  is-universal-Fam-pushout l5 P a p →
  Σ ( hom-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam c (Id (pr1 c a))))
    ( λ h → Id (pr1 h a p) refl)
hom-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout {f = f} {g} c up-X P a p is-univ-P =
  {!!}

is-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout :
  { l1 l2 l3 l4 l5 : Level} {S : UU l1} {A : UU l2} {B : UU l3} {X : UU l5}
  { f : S → A} {g : S → B} (c : cocone f g X) →
  ( up-X : (l : Level) → universal-property-pushout l f g c) →
  ( P : Fam-pushout l4 f g) (a : A) (p : pr1 P a) →
  is-universal-Fam-pushout l5 P a p →
  Σ ( equiv-Fam-pushout P (desc-fam c (Id (pr1 c a))))
    ( λ e → Id (map-equiv (pr1 e a) p) refl)
is-identity-is-universal-Fam-pushout {f = f} {g} c up-X a P p₀ is-eq-P = {!!}
-}</a>
</pre>
